 ek nayaa prashn uth khadaa hua he
 Do i not believe in the existence of God Almighty, omnipresent and omniscient due to any ego?  bijepi or modi ne kaarykram ko chaalu rakhkar ek tarah se sandesh diya ki kam se kam bam blast se aap raajnneetik dal ke kaarykram ko roak nahin sakate

 agar unhone ek line ye kah diya hota ki antkiyon ko majaa chakhaana he, tab uskaa kya parinaam patna or puure desh main us din hota, uski aap kalpana bhi nahin kar sakate

 narendra modi ne us din kam se kam tanaav na bade uske liye koi kasar nahin chodi
 He did not go to the hospital to see the injured, went to Patna Airport and sat with every party leader to ensure that all people return safely to their respective home districts
 baad main mritkon ke parivaar waalon se milane kuch dinon ke baad pahunche
 Therefore, it is useless to compare the two, committing suicide by a farmer in Delhi being fed up with crop wastage and giving a speech after the terror incident
 haa, dilli or patna donon main ek samanta he, wo he donon shaharon or rajya kii police kaa mookadarshak bane rahanaa
 The bomb blasts in Patna are certainly an example of police failure
 gandhi maidan main raily ke ek raat pehle nitish kumaar ne rajya ke police mahanideshak abhayanand ko puure gandhi maidan ko sanitise karne kaa nirdesh diya tha
 But that night a Diwali party was going on in the IPS mess and there was a general perception among the Ala officers of Bihar Police and the officers below them that if they showed more seriousness about the security of Modi's rally, then the martyred political boss means Nitish Kumar will get angry
 
 isliye police ne kahin koi vyavastha nahin kii thi jiske kaaran ek nahin kai bam gandhi maidan main mili or kai blast hue jisamen saat logon kii jaan gai
 The same thing is happening in Delhi
 'aap' kii sabha ho yaa raily, dilli police unhen gambhirtha se nahin leti

 isliye jo intjaam hone chahie wo nahin karte or baad main ek kaagaj media ko li kar dete hai ki kaise 'aap' ke aayojakon ne dilli police kii nahin suni

 2
 Ovary also gets stressed when your ovaries are making eggs, it is called ovulation
